 10/18/1812 Sun 00:00:37  47b5b87437 "Lóbnoe Place, Pierre had so definitely made up his mind that he could no"

 10/18/1812 Sun 00:44:30  a36e0820bb "something... With what? Pierre could not say, and he did not try to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:46:26  5f7245a340 "determine for whom and for what he felt such particular delight in"

 10/18/1812 Sun 00:49:11  cc86f22b60 "sacrifice for; the fact of sacrificing in itself afforded him a new and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:50:31  a0029d9df1 "joyous sensation."
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:51:17  abf0f0a0f1 "CHAPTER XIX"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:53:14  b59fffd306 "On the twenty-fourth of August the battle of the Shevárdino Redoubt was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:54:05  ed064a1a3f "fought, on the twenty-fifth not a shot was fired by either side, and on"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:55:15  c0deace001 "the twenty-sixth the battle of Borodinó itself took place."
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:56:34  2dfa59ee78 "Why and how were the battles of Shevárdino and Borodinó given and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 00:58:29  d955330593 "accepted? Why was the battle of Borodinó fought? There was not the least"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:00:22  304ee9ed5e "sense in it for either the French or the Russians. Its immediate result"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:02:29  172a8c29bf "for the Russians was, and was bound to be, that we were brought nearer"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:04:19  63d0d6b926 "to the destruction of Moscow—which we feared more than anything in"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:05:06  282c5a4601 "the world; and for the French its immediate result was that they were"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:06:15  25a719e42b "brought nearer to the destruction of their whole army—which they feared"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:08:06  99aafeb3d2 "more than anything in the world. What the result must be was quite"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:09:12  542809207f "obvious, and yet Napoleon offered and Kutúzov accepted that battle."
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:10:47  fd8a76e617 "If the commanders had been guided by reason, it would seem that it must"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:12:46  373f7decd1 "have been obvious to Napoleon that by advancing thirteen hundred miles"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:14:30  e7f8564016 "and giving battle with a probability of losing a quarter of his army,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:15:21  3ae95bf2fa "he was advancing to certain destruction, and it must have been equally"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:16:25  0cef24dc0f "clear to Kutúzov that by accepting battle and risking the loss of a"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:17:06  3bffb7d94f "quarter of his army he would certainly lose Moscow. For Kutúzov this was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:17:51  812b39b225 "mathematically clear, as it is that if when playing draughts I have one"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:18:47  10dcc0e2ac "man less and go on exchanging, I shall certainly lose, and therefore"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:20:23  eb060b104a "should not exchange. When my opponent has sixteen men and I have"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:22:00  f303b884b3 "fourteen, I am only one eighth weaker than he, but when I have exchanged"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:24:10  2aed644ccb "thirteen more men he will be three times as strong as I am."
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:25:04  d1d78f82c2 "Before the battle of Borodinó our strength in proportion to the French"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:26:58  8f685c2e38 "was about as five to six, but after that battle it was little more than"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:28:35  1f32d30e40 "one to two: previously we had a hundred thousand against a hundred and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:29:36  aa11bfbdfe "twenty thousand; afterwards little more than fifty thousand against a"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:31:08  dd833be655 "hundred thousand. Yet the shrewd and experienced Kutúzov accepted the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:33:35  fd8ad48c12 "battle, while Napoleon, who was said to be a commander of genius,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:34:44  586d6a3201 "gave it, losing a quarter of his army and lengthening his lines of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:35:35  88d8af1358 "communication still more. If it is said that he expected to end the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:36:15  c302ecebe6 "campaign by occupying Moscow as he had ended a previous campaign by"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:37:57  39a77bb644 "occupying Vienna, there is much evidence to the contrary. Napoleon’s"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:40:26  65f17f3903 "historians themselves tell us that from Smolénsk onwards he wished"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:41:56  c0deace001 "to stop, knew the danger of his extended position, and knew that the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:43:49  61a3484eb0 "occupation of Moscow would not be the end of the campaign, for he had"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:44:56  749a2849e5 "seen at Smolénsk the state in which Russian towns were left to him, and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:47:16  9d3ae47bd9 "had not received a single reply to his repeated announcements of his"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:49:18  0c46ff57d5 "wish to negotiate."
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:50:56  c0deace001 "In giving and accepting battle at Borodinó, Kutúzov acted involuntarily"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:51:34  291b93180b "and irrationally. But later on, to fit what had occurred, the historians"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:52:18  5915d0cf29 "provided cunningly devised evidence of the foresight and genius of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:53:12  06ec18ce84 "generals who, of all the blind tools of history were the most enslaved"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:54:57  f3fb3b7481 "and involuntary."
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:55:54  0c4e4c8ec6 "The ancients have left us model heroic poems in which the heroes furnish"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:57:22  78d8238230 "the whole interest of the story, and we are still unable to accustom"
 10/18/1812 Sun 01:59:18  d407ae7625 "ourselves to the fact that for our epoch histories of that kind are"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:00:30  16eb58533a "meaningless."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:02:16  c8829215fd "On the other question, how the battle of Borodinó and the preceding"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:03:10  f89429b808 "battle of Shevárdino were fought, there also exists a definite and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:05:21  671a4bdb12 "well-known, but quite false, conception. All the historians describe the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:06:40  c1e4d59f8f "affair as follows:"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:07:59  0dc3733a29 "The Russian army, they say, in its retreat from Smolénsk sought out"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:09:34  2111772030 "for itself the best position for a general engagement and found such a"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:12:00  fc1312acbc "position at Borodinó."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:13:42  24ec808a77 "The Russians, they say, fortified this position in advance on the left"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:14:12  4668bef8a3 "of the highroad (from Moscow to Smolénsk) and almost at a right angle"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:16:27  eb2e9498e8 "to it, from Borodinó to Utítsa, at the very place where the battle was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:18:41  1d6b6f682c "fought."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:19:24  b9094bfead "In front of this position, they say, a fortified outpost was set up on"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:21:49  4e7bbf56ab "the Shevárdino mound to observe the enemy. On the twenty-fourth, we"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:23:15  9bf6cf3634 "are told, Napoleon attacked this advanced post and took it, and, on the"

 10/18/1812 Sun 02:25:15  d16a72c551 "the field of Borodinó."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:27:18  116a772dd0 "So the histories say, and it is all quite wrong, as anyone who cares to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:29:16  06a45b96aa "look into the matter can easily convince himself."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:31:10  cd35811209 "The Russians did not seek out the best position but, on the contrary,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:32:55  0b271fd625 "during the retreat passed many positions better than Borodinó. They did"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:34:25  dd92c98854 "not stop at any one of these positions because Kutúzov did not wish to"

 10/18/1812 Sun 02:36:17  ed9232a18e "for a battle had not yet expressed itself strongly enough, and because"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:37:47  c0deace001 "Milorádovich had not yet arrived with the militia, and for many other"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:38:52  60bad41328 "reasons. The fact is that other positions they had passed were stronger,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:39:29  e9dcc99ae3 "and that the position at Borodinó (the one where the battle was fought),"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:40:57  06c9ad215e "far from being strong, was no more a position than any other spot one"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:42:53  988d61d9f4 "might find in the Russian Empire by sticking a pin into the map at"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:44:49  f27764c69d "hazard."
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:46:51  912c2f99bc "Not only did the Russians not fortify the position on the field of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:48:03  c0deace001 "Borodinó to the left of, and at a right angle to, the highroad (that"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:49:46  d3df6a6e10 "is, the position on which the battle took place), but never till the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:51:47  30e4b2d641 "twenty-fifth of August, 1812, did they think that a battle might be"

 10/18/1812 Sun 02:53:36  b06e5d74b0 "entrenchments there by the twenty fifth and that those begun on the"

 10/18/1812 Sun 02:57:39  9ae891ea88 "position of the Shevárdino Redoubt. That redoubt was quite senseless"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:58:11  80fc53083c "in front of the position where the battle was accepted. Why was it"
 10/18/1812 Sun 02:59:37  cc6b488d11 "more strongly fortified than any other post? And why were all efforts"

 10/18/1812 Sun 03:12:26  c013f6b7d2 "himself in his report, written in hot haste after the battle, speaks of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:14:01  3ca62cadb8 "the Shevárdino Redoubt as the left flank of the position. It was much"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:15:12  ba6b984282 "later, when reports on the battle of Borodinó were written at leisure,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:17:03  75687c91ee "that the incorrect and extraordinary statement was invented (probably to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:18:49  d1b8b544c0 "justify the mistakes of a commander in chief who had to be represented"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:20:52  083eaedd6e "as infallible) that the Shevárdino Redoubt was an advanced post—whereas"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:21:22  e577e5e9fb "in reality it was simply a fortified point on the left flank—and that"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:23:43  e6c35ec83f "the battle of Borodinó was fought by us on an entrenched position"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:25:54  7e288a9559 "previously selected, whereas it was fought on a quite unexpected spot"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:27:22  a269303335 "which was almost unentrenched."
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:29:09  c5ad09005b "The case was evidently this: a position was selected along the river"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:30:46  399c256dd7 "Kolochá—which crosses the highroad not at a right angle but at an acute"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:31:38  7d5da20beb "angle—so that the left flank was at Shevárdino, the right flank near the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:34:00  eb2ef494eb "village of Nóvoe, and the center at Borodinó at the confluence of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:35:19  40055fb0ff "rivers Kolochá and Vóyna."
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:37:24  097b519426 "To anyone who looks at the field of Borodinó without thinking of how"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:39:09  e93eab754d "the battle was actually fought, this position, protected by the river"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:41:00  c0deace001 "Kolochá, presents itself as obvious for an army whose object was to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:42:05  98a97ac4a7 "prevent an enemy from advancing along the Smolénsk road to Moscow."
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:43:40  b470ba6040 "Napoleon, riding to Valúevo on the twenty-fourth, did not see (as the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:45:42  a8d01fd364 "history books say he did) the position of the Russians from Utítsa"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:47:35  14272b8e50 "to Borodinó (he could not have seen that position because it did not"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:48:38  985698059d "exist), nor did he see an advanced post of the Russian army, but while"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:50:56  c0deace001 "pursuing the Russian rearguard he came upon the left flank of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:52:23  8853aea730 "Russian position—at the Shevárdino Redoubt—and unexpectedly for the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:52:54  6270d42320 "Russians moved his army across the Kolochá. And the Russians, not having"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:55:03  c4fcb9a492 "time to begin a general engagement, withdrew their left wing from the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:56:11  ffb091f4d0 "position they had intended to occupy and took up a new position which"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:58:23  f1d2ce4cd7 "had not been foreseen and was not fortified. By crossing to the other"
 10/18/1812 Sun 03:59:20  12f0d3881a "side of the Kolochá to the left of the highroad, Napoleon shifted the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:01:33  d28e995e0e "whole forthcoming battle from right to left (looking from the Russian"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:02:18  175609428c "side) and transferred it to the plain between Utítsa, Semënovsk, and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:04:36  363f4fd672 "Borodinó—a plain no more advantageous as a position than any other plain"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:05:57  6357ab0866 "in Russia—and there the whole battle of the twenty-sixth of August took"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:08:15  7c4729271f "place."
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:10:25  8a0b1bf213 "Had Napoleon not ridden out on the evening of the twenty-fourth to the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:11:38  7f628b4d2b "Kolochá, and had he not then ordered an immediate attack on the redoubt"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:13:29  70cce8b8db "but had begun the attack next morning, no one would have doubted that"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:14:29  98bf19d952 "the Shevárdino Redoubt was the left flank of our position, and the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:16:51  caebabe620 "battle would have taken place where we expected it. In that case"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:17:41  3fb58d27be "we should probably have defended the Shevárdino Redoubt—our left"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:19:03  53490e7caf "flank—still more obstinately. We should have attacked Napoleon in the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:21:17  31caa51bce "center or on the right, and the engagement would have taken place on the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:22:57  b11f752977 "twenty-fifth, in the position we intended and had fortified. But as the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:23:46  7afa287888 "attack on our left flank took place in the evening after the retreat of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:25:08  f950013238 "our rear guard (that is, immediately after the fight at Gridnëva), and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:26:09  5b50ee29a9 "as the Russian commanders did not wish, or were not in time, to begin a"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:28:27  f428f25bd1 "general engagement then on the evening of the twenty-fourth, the first"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:30:24  fab50cb348 "and chief action of the battle of Borodinó was already lost on the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:32:30  5c2fb02bf0 "twenty-fourth, and obviously led to the loss of the one fought on the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:34:20  c0deace001 "twenty-sixth."
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:34:51  3b81c6ebbb "After the loss of the Shevárdino Redoubt, we found ourselves on the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:36:21  4800d13166 "morning of the twenty-fifth without a position for our left flank, and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:37:41  f8a7d85a21 "were forced to bend it back and hastily entrench it where it chanced to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:39:01  7f1021f509 "be."
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:40:24  90644b43f2 "Not only was the Russian army on the twenty-sixth defended by weak,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:41:15  acce8b29d8 "unfinished entrenchments, but the disadvantage of that position was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:43:13  5bd722f789 "increased by the fact that the Russian commanders—not having fully"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:44:18  bf0bad530f "realized what had happened, namely the loss of our position on the left"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:45:28  dcfc34e675 "flank and the shifting of the whole field of the forthcoming battle from"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:47:10  3c24fa078c "right to left—maintained their extended position from the village of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:48:22  b049ce9fd1 "Nóvoe to Utítsa, and consequently had to move their forces from right to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:49:20  6b4d13c01d "left during the battle. So it happened that throughout the whole battle"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:49:53  577779a1c0 "the Russians opposed the entire French army launched against our left"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:50:46  fe2c9a9b88 "flank with but half as many men. (Poniatowski’s action against Utítsa,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:51:16  5c9bbe53bc "and Uvárov’s on the right flank against the French, were actions"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:52:24  088965deb7 "distinct from the main course of the battle.) So the battle of Borodinó"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:54:38  1a0cce8ff1 "did not take place at all as (in an effort to conceal our commanders’"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:55:38  37056cbea4 "mistakes even at the cost of diminishing the glory due to the Russian"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:56:31  30fd026439 "army and people) it has been described. The battle of Borodinó was not"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:57:06  a15e43986c "fought on a chosen and entrenched position with forces only slightly"
 10/18/1812 Sun 04:58:50  2f8ab1200e "weaker than those of the enemy, but, as a result of the loss of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:01:19  c0deace001 "Shevárdino Redoubt, the Russians fought the battle of Borodinó on an"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:03:14  ca62d5ccef "open and almost unentrenched position, with forces only half as numerous"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:04:35  70e0c1a942 "as the French; that is to say, under conditions in which it was not"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:06:43  310893eb87 "merely unthinkable to fight for ten hours and secure an indecisive"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:08:26  148db94f67 "result, but unthinkable to keep an army even from complete"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:09:06  be4bfff862 "disintegration and flight."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:10:42  4caa863d80 "CHAPTER XX"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:11:38  b73ea9a630 "On the morning of the twenty-fifth Pierre was leaving Mozháysk. At the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:13:01  b385df037f "descent of the high steep hill, down which a winding road led out of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:14:38  c34d2b28cd "town past the cathedral on the right, where a service was being held and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:16:26  1b507370ca "the bells were ringing, Pierre got out of his vehicle and proceeded on"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:18:31  8781c36004 "foot. Behind him a cavalry regiment was coming down the hill preceded by"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:20:58  be5008f461 "its singers. Coming up toward him was a train of carts carrying men who"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:21:40  d68757bdd2 "had been wounded in the engagement the day before. The peasant drivers,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:24:06  f78c738bfb "shouting and lashing their horses, kept crossing from side to side. The"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:26:01  535bcd2506 "carts, in each of which three or four wounded soldiers were lying"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:27:10  a9f43a0f35 "or sitting, jolted over the stones that had been thrown on the steep"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:28:16  de04be482e "incline to make it something like a road. The wounded, bandaged with"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:29:15  7258c44c61 "rags, with pale cheeks, compressed lips, and knitted brows, held on to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:31:07  e6b3e37a0f "the sides of the carts as they were jolted against one another. Almost"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:32:33  c3fb36522e "all of them stared with naïve, childlike curiosity at Pierre’s white hat"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:33:28  30d630694b "and green swallow-tail coat."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:35:43  10ec911a7e "Pierre’s coachman shouted angrily at the convoy of wounded to keep to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:37:01  a5ac1672a1 "one side of the road. The cavalry regiment, as it descended the hill"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:38:26  5b803268fa "with its singers, surrounded Pierre’s carriage and blocked the road."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:40:17  71dcc5409d "Pierre stopped, being pressed against the side of the cutting in which"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:41:57  73fa6447ef "the road ran. The sunshine from behind the hill did not penetrate into"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:43:45  076b9a76b1 "the cutting and there it was cold and damp, but above Pierre’s head was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:45:33  6c05fc6f67 "the bright August sunshine and the bells sounded merrily. One of the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:46:27  f063d61992 "carts with wounded stopped by the side of the road close to Pierre. The"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:48:07  7cbc45a11f "driver in his bast shoes ran panting up to it, placed a stone under one"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:49:02  d04ca7ed5c "of its tireless hind wheels, and began arranging the breech-band on his"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:51:13  a14cb4598b "little horse."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:51:44  47e0ce1153 "One of the wounded, an old soldier with a bandaged arm who was following"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:54:09  180f8d4075 "the cart on foot, caught hold of it with his sound hand and turned to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:55:25  a396f951dc "look at Pierre."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:55:59  131186a3aa "“I say, fellow countryman! Will they set us down here or take us on to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:57:30  955dba0cef "Moscow?” he asked."
 10/18/1812 Sun 05:59:12  85b0d51ec1 "Pierre was so deep in thought that he did not hear the question. He was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:00:39  8b9636315d "looking now at the cavalry regiment that had met the convoy of wounded,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:01:17  c0deace001 "now at the cart by which he was standing, in which two wounded men"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:02:11  8f8360b478 "were sitting and one was lying. One of those sitting up in the cart had"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:04:38  8ec6c5ae1e "probably been wounded in the cheek. His whole head was wrapped in rags"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:05:51  23e37a0631 "and one cheek was swollen to the size of a baby’s head. His nose"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:06:41  14b5dc2877 "and mouth were twisted to one side. This soldier was looking at the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:08:26  501a44c9ab "cathedral and crossing himself. Another, a young lad, a fair-haired"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:10:18  8f396f9d64 "recruit as white as though there was no blood in his thin face, looked"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:11:36  8a5855c6a7 "at Pierre kindly, with a fixed smile. The third lay prone so that his"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:13:42  e1ca0ec5e1 "face was not visible. The cavalry singers were passing close by:"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:14:48  e17081a95e "   Ah lost, quite lost... is my head so keen,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:16:54  c0deace001 "   Living in a foreign land..."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:17:37  57149f3c03 "they sang their soldiers’ dance song."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:18:31  d34066892c "As if responding to them but with a different sort of merriment, the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:19:50  d66663ffc3 "metallic sound of the bells reverberated high above and the hot rays of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:21:55  631ff206f5 "the sun bathed the top of the opposite slope with yet another sort of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:23:59  5ccfdd678e "merriment. But beneath the slope, by the cart with the wounded near the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:24:36  f6d227c53d "panting little nag where Pierre stood, it was damp, somber, and sad."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:25:59  9ae65562d0 "The soldier with the swollen cheek looked angrily at the cavalry"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:28:19  ce10c2fa77 "singers."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:29:58  1760e65cba "“Oh, the coxcombs!” he muttered reproachfully."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:31:39  57a574e7be "“It’s not the soldiers only, but I’ve seen peasants today, too...."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:33:40  b0b77598ce "The peasants—even they have to go,” said the soldier behind the cart,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:35:21  4d401a64a7 "addressing Pierre with a sad smile. “No distinctions made nowadays...."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:36:57  4e9045d767 "They want the whole nation to fall on them—in a word, it’s Moscow! They"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:37:44  29d81b140d "want to make an end of it.”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:39:29  9d4b83cea9 "In spite of the obscurity of the soldier’s words Pierre understood what"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:39:59  ef4073624f "he wanted to say and nodded approval."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:41:51  498cff4736 "The road was clear again; Pierre descended the hill and drove on."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:42:25  803453f401 "He kept looking to either side of the road for familiar faces, but only"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:43:03  43a9f33c78 "saw everywhere the unfamiliar faces of various military men of different"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:45:26  bf955de611 "branches of the service, who all looked with astonishment at his white"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:46:24  e3b29a54bc "hat and green tail coat."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:48:52  2e7962b698 "Having gone nearly three miles he at last met an acquaintance and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:49:50  8a7ec847e6 "eagerly addressed him. This was one of the head army doctors. He was"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:51:00  1568c86dba "driving toward Pierre in a covered gig, sitting beside a young surgeon,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:52:35  dbcf5f1de7 "and on recognizing Pierre he told the Cossack who occupied the driver’s"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:54:55  47f0a58712 "seat to pull up."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:56:45  c0deace001 "“Count! Your excellency, how come you to be here?” asked the doctor."
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:57:34  47d6a82185 "“Well, you know, I wanted to see...”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 06:59:00  a52154ecaa "“Yes, yes, there will be something to see....”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:00:13  32dfd457ec "Pierre got out and talked to the doctor, explaining his intention of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:01:15  078f516831 "taking part in a battle."
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:02:57  fde0b6f5f6 "The doctor advised him to apply direct to Kutúzov."
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:04:59  d0e042369f "“Why should you be God knows where out of sight, during the battle?” he"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:08:36  d35d97fe2f "Highness knows you and will receive you graciously. That’s what you must"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:10:37  1fa916e7ba "do.”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:11:52  483223c760 "The doctor seemed tired and in a hurry."
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:12:50  31bb7fe279 "“You think so?... Ah, I also wanted to ask you where our position is"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:14:01  c0deace001 "exactly?” said Pierre."
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:16:22  ace817c7ee "“The position?” repeated the doctor. “Well, that’s not my line. Drive"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:18:36  462f3f6802 "past Tatárinova, a lot of digging is going on there. Go up the hillock"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:20:00  c0deace001 "and you’ll see.”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:21:21  4127ffaa0f "“Can one see from there?... If you would...”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:22:45  6e2712a4f2 "But the doctor interrupted him and moved toward his gig."
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:24:45  e21a58da75 "“I would go with you but on my honor I’m up to here”—and he pointed to"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:29:20  b5b3ebd0ee "of a hundred thousand we must expect at least twenty thousand wounded,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:31:05  79f6e161cb "and we haven’t stretchers, or bunks, or dressers, or doctors enough for"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:34:41  55ac18db2b "well—we must manage as best we can!”"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:36:58  702128c385 "The strange thought that of the thousands of men, young and old, who"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:39:26  e7133f1540 "had stared with merry surprise at his hat (perhaps the very men he had"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:41:22  a6012cdc85 "noticed), twenty thousand were inevitably doomed to wounds and death"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:44:00  74934be6b6 "“They may die tomorrow; why are they thinking of anything but death?”"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:51:03  541d6eed33 "“The cavalry ride to battle and meet the wounded and do not for a moment"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:56:26  fa423fdfab "In front of a landowner’s house to the left of the road stood carriages,"

 10/18/1812 Sun 07:58:22  2bd09615b6 "was putting up there, but just when Pierre arrived he was not in and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 07:58:57  7b12f92c77 "hardly any of the staff were there—they had gone to the church service."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:00:10  120d364eb8 "Pierre drove on toward Górki."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:01:22  34a1d78fca "When he had ascended the hill and reached the little village street, he"

 10/18/1812 Sun 08:10:49  a4616ac14f "Some of them were digging, others were wheeling barrowloads of earth"

 10/18/1812 Sun 08:27:06  32d757c646 "than anything he had yet seen or heard."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:28:08  e8ab446739 "CHAPTER XXI"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:29:51  a89a5369a7 "Pierre stepped out of his carriage and, passing the toiling militiamen,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:31:58  c0deace001 "ascended the knoll from which, according to the doctor, the battlefield"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:33:50  81e9fa0e54 "could be seen."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:34:56  d826e01869 "It was about eleven o’clock. The sun shone somewhat to the left and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:35:35  fffb09d1ad "behind him and brightly lit up the enormous panorama which, rising like"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:37:28  aef14b0830 "an amphitheater, extended before him in the clear rarefied atmosphere."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:38:11  c0deace001 "From above on the left, bisecting that amphitheater, wound the Smolénsk"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:38:58  bfc9db28a7 "highroad, passing through a village with a white church some five"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:39:38  d50ec9850a "hundred paces in front of the knoll and below it. This was Borodinó."
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:40:54  c973278bb8 "Below the village the road crossed the river by a bridge and, winding"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:42:15  f19f301950 "down and up, rose higher and higher to the village of Valúevo visible"
 10/18/1812 Sun 08:44:43  61853adcbb "about four miles away, where Napoleon was then stationed. Beyond Valúevo"

 10/18/1812 Sun 08:58:06  0d37ba7eef "grain, and the smoking ruins of Semënovsk, which had been burned down,"

 10/18/1812 Sun 09:01:00  a74633ae7a "All that Pierre saw was so indefinite that neither the left nor the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 09:03:29  26848f3bd6 "right side of the field fully satisfied his expectations. Nowhere"

 10/18/1812 Sun 09:05:44  ab08f80177 "meadows, troops, woods, the smoke of campfires, villages, mounds, and"

 10/18/1812 Sun 15:26:07  522adac142 "CHAPTER XXIII"
 10/18/1812 Sun 15:27:42  27d70b2ea4 "From Górki, Bennigsen descended the highroad to the bridge which, when"

 10/18/1812 Sun 16:15:57  e17effaf8f "From the flèches they rode still farther to the left, along a road"

 10/18/1812 Sun 16:29:16  44ab41fc7c "Here, at the extreme left flank, Bennigsen talked a great deal and with"

 10/18/1812 Sun 16:57:42  6c19f7a995 "CHAPTER XXIV"
 10/18/1812 Sun 16:58:15  c0deace001 "On that bright evening of August 25, Prince Andrew lay leaning on his"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:00:39  e0becfd888 "elbow in a broken-down shed in the village of Knyazkóvo at the further"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:01:44  f17ad1ebb6 "end of his regiment’s encampment. Through a gap in the broken wall he"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:03:17  fad0ef1d66 "could see, beside the wooden fence, a row of thirty-year-old birches"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:05:04  27b6571990 "with their lower branches lopped off, a field on which shocks of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:05:50  76066f78ef "oats were standing, and some bushes near which rose the smoke of"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:08:13  f61db1a3db "campfires—the soldiers’ kitchens."
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:10:31  e8c3806766 "Narrow and burdensome and useless to anyone as his life now seemed to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:11:30  465d0ecf04 "him, Prince Andrew on the eve of battle felt agitated and irritable as"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:13:03  c8819558fd "he had done seven years before at Austerlitz."
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:14:43  54a28d0aad "He had received and given the orders for next day’s battle and had"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:17:12  b4e8166e20 "nothing more to do. But his thoughts—the simplest, clearest, and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:19:19  55c89d592c "therefore most terrible thoughts—would give him no peace. He knew that"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:21:18  90d020a5eb "tomorrow’s battle would be the most terrible of all he had taken"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:22:14  097ffb7f86 "part in, and for the first time in his life the possibility of death"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:24:36  ff34b43907 "presented itself to him—not in relation to any worldly matter or with"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:26:14  a5b2489aa1 "reference to its effect on others, but simply in relation to himself, to"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:27:21  bda04c3ff6 "his own soul—vividly, plainly, terribly, and almost as a certainty. And"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:27:53  1306bbe699 "from the height of this perception all that had previously tormented and"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:29:25  cea49ba67e "preoccupied him suddenly became illumined by a cold white light without"

 10/18/1812 Sun 17:32:50  ce0d96cb37 "appeared to him like magic-lantern pictures at which he had long been"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:35:12  b52a97bfc7 "gazing by artificial light through a glass. Now he suddenly saw those"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:36:15  097713deee "badly daubed pictures in clear daylight and without a glass. “Yes,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:38:32  bc3686aa0a "yes! There they are, those false images that agitated, enraptured,"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:39:29  358b3f8fe3 "and tormented me,” said he to himself, passing in review the principal"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:41:46  0c1f6ddb9a "pictures of the magic lantern of life and regarding them now in the cold"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:42:46  872b6528cd "white daylight of his clear perception of death. “There they are, those"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:44:21  d96a77fb7d "rudely painted figures that once seemed splendid and mysterious."
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:45:35  30eeca93d1 "Glory, the good of society, love of a woman, the Fatherland itself—how"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:46:30  d340186647 "important these pictures appeared to me, with what profound meaning they"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:48:43  32ff2641d2 "seemed to be filled! And it is all so simple, pale, and crude in the"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:49:51  d56eed0849 "cold white light of this morning which I feel is dawning for me.” The"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:51:22  cf71667d6e "three great sorrows of his life held his attention in particular: his"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:52:39  1ca9507d44 "love for a woman, his father’s death, and the French invasion which had"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:55:04  2e97b4a610 "overrun half Russia. “Love... that little girl who seemed to me brimming"
 10/18/1812 Sun 17:56:43  dc7f26ecc0 "over with mystic forces! Yes, indeed, I loved her. I made romantic plans"

 10/18/1812 Sun 18:06:56  99d38414af "“When my father built Bald Hills he thought the place was his: his"

 10/18/1812 Sun 18:13:19  c0deace001 "it is a trial sent from above. What is the trial for, when he is not"
 10/18/1812 Sun 18:14:40  6abb9b108f "here and will never return? He is not here! For whom then is the trial"
 10/18/1812 Sun 18:15:27  41616e9cf4 "intended? The Fatherland, the destruction of Moscow! And tomorrow I"
 10/18/1812 Sun 18:17:10  fc73d6d643 "shall be killed, perhaps not even by a Frenchman but by one of our own"

 10/18/1812 Sun 19:16:34  b39c7deb6e "CHAPTER XXV"

 10/19/1812 Mon 01:16:07  454f2209f2 "It was already dark, and Pierre could not make out whether the"

 10/19/1812 Mon 02:04:43  8b2f4e42bf "CHAPTER XXVI"
 10/19/1812 Mon 02:05:41  00ea843133 "On August 25, the eve of the battle of Borodinó, M. de Beausset, prefect"
 10/19/1812 Mon 02:07:21  f763b95658 "of the French Emperor’s palace, arrived at Napoleon’s quarters at"
 10/19/1812 Mon 02:08:52  f46f838767 "Valúevo with Colonel Fabvier, the former from Paris and the latter from"

 10/19/1812 Mon 02:17:19  03475a732d "The Emperor Napoleon had not yet left his bedroom and was finishing his"

 10/19/1812 Mon 05:40:33  f3b6c7c100 "CHAPTER XXVII"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:41:22  71abda8dda "On the twenty-fifth of August, so his historians tell us, Napoleon spent"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:42:25  4f3704f37d "the whole day on horseback inspecting the locality, considering plans"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:44:18  3d6c4e7d53 "submitted to him by his marshals, and personally giving commands to his"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:46:32  c0deace001 "generals."
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:47:23  0151332b17 "The original line of the Russian forces along the river Kolochá had"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:49:46  a281abfde6 "been dislocated by the capture of the Shevárdino Redoubt on the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:50:30  bd27fc32d9 "twenty-fourth, and part of the line—the left flank—had been drawn back."
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:51:48  d3b624d355 "That part of the line was not entrenched and in front of it the ground"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:53:07  e91469b6ac "was more open and level than elsewhere. It was evident to anyone,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:54:21  a547a30a58 "military or not, that it was here the French should attack. It would"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:55:54  25bb65fdfa "seem that not much consideration was needed to reach this conclusion,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 05:57:57  5ed9427e07 "nor any particular care or trouble on the part of the Emperor and his"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:00:12  eb8507caad "marshals, nor was there any need of that special and supreme quality"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:01:28  7784ffb0cc "called genius that people are so apt to ascribe to Napoleon; yet the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:02:51  0a04a4fd91 "historians who described the event later and the men who then surrounded"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:04:10  337bfb1fc9 "Napoleon, and he himself, thought otherwise."
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:04:51  9310b7227f "Napoleon rode over the plain and surveyed the locality with a profound"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:06:17  0a3dde73fb "air and in silence, nodded with approval or shook his head dubiously,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:08:16  672575e096 "and without communicating to the generals around him the profound"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:09:28  6b6a931634 "course of ideas which guided his decisions merely gave them his final"

 10/19/1812 Mon 06:16:06  1a3958607a "why not. To a proposal made by General Campan (who was to attack the"

 10/19/1812 Mon 06:19:19  1c7ec46e0c "the so-called Duke of Elchingen (Ney) ventured to remark that a movement"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:20:41  f553d28335 "through the woods was dangerous and might disorder the division."
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:22:51  f772f907dc "Having inspected the country opposite the Shevárdino Redoubt, Napoleon"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:24:15  782db879f7 "pondered a little in silence and then indicated the spots where two"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:26:29  da9c19466c "batteries should be set up by the morrow to act against the Russian"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:28:50  36cc68003b "entrenchments, and the places where, in line with them, the field"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:30:47  603f7a11a1 "artillery should be placed."
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:32:24  a483f4b73a "After giving these and other commands he returned to his tent, and the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:34:29  e3df05c546 "dispositions for the battle were written down from his dictation."
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:36:23  98d66ed2d0 "These dispositions, of which the French historians write with enthusiasm"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:38:14  3596e6ac96 "and other historians with profound respect, were as follows:"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:40:13  1d0d51408d "At dawn the two new batteries established during the night on the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:42:13  8b531193d7 "plain occupied by the Prince d’Eckmühl will open fire on the opposing"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:42:52  4de5fc990b "batteries of the enemy."
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:43:32  c0deace001 "At the same time the commander of the artillery of the 1st Corps,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 06:45:06  fe3e676207 "General Pernetti, with thirty cannon of Campan’s division and all the"

 10/19/1812 Mon 08:16:33  c0deace001 "and come into line with the rest of the forces."
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:19:01  24b01a610e "As far as one can make out, not so much from this unintelligible"

 10/19/1812 Mon 08:48:45  f04acfd706 "CHAPTER XXVIII"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:51:08  3becde2717 "Many historians say that the French did not win the battle of Borodinó"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:53:22  48a1c53827 "because Napoleon had a cold, and that if he had not had a cold the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:54:23  577bb2500a "orders he gave before and during the battle would have been still more"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:56:12  9d8d56084a "full of genius and Russia would have been lost and the face of the world"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:57:12  573f4e2562 "have been changed. To historians who believe that Russia was shaped"
 10/19/1812 Mon 08:59:12  656b6df080 "by the will of one man—Peter the Great—and that France from a republic"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:00:37  61a985f28d "became an empire and French armies went to Russia at the will of one"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:02:19  0876ee4034 "man—Napoleon—to say that Russia remained a power because Napoleon had a"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:03:16  c741eed255 "bad cold on the twenty-fourth of August may seem logical and convincing."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:04:20  c0deace001 "If it had depended on Napoleon’s will to fight or not to fight the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:05:15  6cb5d06452 "battle of Borodinó, and if this or that other arrangement depended on"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:05:47  384c4b7c3f "his will, then evidently a cold affecting the manifestation of his will"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:07:57  1143b2bb26 "might have saved Russia, and consequently the valet who omitted to bring"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:09:34  af3e279168 "Napoleon his waterproof boots on the twenty-fourth would have been"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:11:58  8255fb3743 "the savior of Russia. Along that line of thought such a deduction is"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:14:02  a705b2988b "indubitable, as indubitable as the deduction Voltaire made in jest"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:14:44  2363759353 "(without knowing what he was jesting at) when he saw that the Massacre"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:16:27  90bb58d8c9 "of St. Bartholomew was due to Charles IX’s stomach being deranged. But"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:17:12  3f48c3a8ee "to men who do not admit that Russia was formed by the will of one man,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:17:50  5ec34266ef "Peter I, or that the French Empire was formed and the war with Russia"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:18:33  33214fab7b "begun by the will of one man, Napoleon, that argument seems not merely"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:20:27  199c4afbee "untrue and irrational, but contrary to all human reality. To the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:22:56  005d773758 "question of what causes historic events another answer presents itself,"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:23:34  849ea339e1 "namely, that the course of human events is predetermined from on"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:24:47  9a609c2da3 "high—depends on the coincidence of the wills of all who take part in the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:25:58  5bb34eae0d "events, and that a Napoleon’s influence on the course of these events is"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:27:33  d10e24f679 "purely external and fictitious."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:29:46  9827a435aa "Strange as at first glance it may seem to suppose that the Massacre of"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:30:27  4a3453a615 "St. Bartholomew was not due to Charles IX’s will, though he gave the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:31:21  0efa4eef31 "order for it and thought it was done as a result of that order; and"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:33:28  03b797b172 "strange as it may seem to suppose that the slaughter of eighty thousand"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:35:45  ed0119542f "men at Borodinó was not due to Napoleon’s will, though he ordered the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:37:10  d7e850d150 "commencement and conduct of the battle and thought it was done"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:38:28  b96519b82b "because he ordered it; strange as these suppositions appear, yet human"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:39:16  effce7c89d "dignity—which tells me that each of us is, if not more at least not less"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:40:12  9d096bb4b1 "a man than the great Napoleon—demands the acceptance of that solution of"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:42:25  8396538c39 "the question, and historic investigation abundantly confirms it."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:44:25  5739a5c4b0 "At the battle of Borodinó Napoleon shot at no one and killed no one."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:45:48  7b40da71ac "That was all done by the soldiers. Therefore it was not he who killed"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:46:28  c0deace001 "people."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:48:08  4adbc7b409 "The French soldiers went to kill and be killed at the battle of Borodinó"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:48:50  73484670ec "not because of Napoleon’s orders but by their own volition. The whole"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:50:43  efe0badc36 "army—French, Italian, German, Polish, and Dutch—hungry, ragged, and"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:51:22  9105783c16 "weary of the campaign, felt at the sight of an army blocking their road"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:53:50  075347cbcd "to Moscow that the wine was drawn and must be drunk. Had Napoleon then"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:55:10  d06daff2e4 "forbidden them to fight the Russians, they would have killed him and"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:56:02  dbf672232e "have proceeded to fight the Russians because it was inevitable."
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:57:36  f8b71042aa "When they heard Napoleon’s proclamation offering them, as compensation"
 10/19/1812 Mon 09:59:11  db3508080d "for mutilation and death, the words of posterity about their having been"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:00:03  f7b175a04f "in the battle before Moscow, they cried “Vive l’Empereur!” just as they"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:01:42  3e4986c4a7 "had cried “Vive l’Empereur!” at the sight of the portrait of the boy"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:02:33  1939fa4ae7 "piercing the terrestrial globe with a toy stick, and just as they would"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:03:24  c7759348e7 "have cried “Vive l’Empereur!” at any nonsense that might be told them."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:05:11  94bbf81b99 "There was nothing left for them to do but cry “Vive l’Empereur!” and go"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:06:37  4771b6086a "to fight, in order to get food and rest as conquerors in Moscow. So it"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:08:01  c0deace001 "was not because of Napoleon’s commands that they killed their fellow"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:09:11  5b417030df "men."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:10:46  b359cb459c "And it was not Napoleon who directed the course of the battle, for none"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:12:03  a1e81542be "of his orders were executed and during the battle he did not know what"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:12:42  510c883dba "was going on before him. So the way in which these people killed one"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:13:57  dbbcf86245 "another was not decided by Napoleon’s will but occurred independently of"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:16:01  b57c73da4d "him, in accord with the will of hundreds of thousands of people who took"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:17:28  46c6bab25c "part in the common action. It only seemed to Napoleon that it all took"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:19:01  c0deace001 "place by his will. And so the question whether he had or had not a"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:20:04  c3acaa6d65 "cold has no more historic interest than the cold of the least of the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:20:59  460f669dac "transport soldiers."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:22:06  c96010deda "Moreover, the assertion made by various writers that his cold was"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:23:11  9d892a83a8 "the cause of his dispositions not being as well-planned as on former"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:23:42  91148d8b76 "occasions, and of his orders during the battle not being as good as"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:25:59  751671c834 "previously, is quite baseless, which again shows that Napoleon’s cold on"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:27:08  c6c45de250 "the twenty-sixth of August was unimportant."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:28:54  5aee39ac27 "The dispositions cited above are not at all worse, but are even"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:31:21  93bb20be1f "better, than previous dispositions by which he had won victories. His"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:32:28  bb6651b44f "pseudo-orders during the battle were also no worse than formerly, but"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:33:04  eed27dbabe "much the same as usual. These dispositions and orders only seem worse"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:33:45  3edeceae92 "than previous ones because the battle of Borodinó was the first Napoleon"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:35:48  7b705d2761 "did not win. The profoundest and most excellent dispositions and orders"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:37:21  975986fdc2 "seem very bad, and every learned militarist criticizes them with looks"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:38:24  781e82babe "of importance, when they relate to a battle that has been lost, and the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:39:36  c0deace001 "very worst dispositions and orders seem very good, and serious people"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:41:00  c12626ccfe "fill whole volumes to demonstrate their merits, when they relate to a"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:43:29  ccc5b88e21 "battle that has been won."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:44:12  14cdaf74e0 "The dispositions drawn up by Weyrother for the battle of Austerlitz were"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:46:22  b2c049bbae "a model of perfection for that kind of composition, but still they were"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:47:06  05be9077df "criticized—criticized for their very perfection, for their excessive"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:48:29  1230c1b10a "minuteness."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:49:36  92f2c40fd3 "Napoleon at the battle of Borodinó fulfilled his office as"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:51:07  af87f76b6b "representative of authority as well as, and even better than, at other"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:52:31  5fe80b5ef6 "battles. He did nothing harmful to the progress of the battle; he"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:54:23  068ecca562 "inclined to the most reasonable opinions, he made no confusion, did not"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:55:20  ffc2074ae2 "contradict himself, did not get frightened or run away from the field of"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:57:41  4d8c0ab812 "battle, but with his great tact and military experience carried out his"
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:58:28  baf89a88fa "role of appearing to command, calmly and with dignity."
 10/19/1812 Mon 10:59:18  7eed360d61 "CHAPTER XXIX"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:00:04  834dbc00cc "On returning from a second inspection of the lines, Napoleon remarked:"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:01:17  c2bcf67d70 "“The chessmen are set up, the game will begin tomorrow!”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:02:44  9010880b28 "Having ordered punch and summoned de Beausset, he began to talk to him"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:04:05  9d3e510fc8 "about Paris and about some changes he meant to make in the Empress’"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:05:11  52ab5bef72 "household, surprising the prefect by his memory of minute details"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:06:26  a691f89bf1 "relating to the court."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:08:26  f0715e7c8e "He showed an interest in trifles, joked about de Beausset’s love of"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:10:48  b5f293441b "travel, and chatted carelessly, as a famous, self-confident surgeon who"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:12:00  a640b2b004 "knows his job does when turning up his sleeves and putting on his apron"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:12:30  3c889c13f5 "while a patient is being strapped to the operating table. “The matter is"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:14:59  a10e2bcecf "in my hands and is clear and definite in my head. When the time comes to"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:16:14  79f97de4d1 "set to work I shall do it as no one else could, but now I can jest, and"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:18:17  9de96ed84c "the more I jest and the calmer I am the more tranquil and confident you"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:19:49  c3826b9691 "ought to be, and the more amazed at my genius.”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:21:37  cda71b4689 "Having finished his second glass of punch, Napoleon went to rest before"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:22:23  9b7d0a0619 "the serious business which, he considered, awaited him next day. He"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:23:12  0e927f3d42 "was so much interested in that task that he was unable to sleep, and"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:23:54  b9b8d2c666 "in spite of his cold which had grown worse from the dampness of the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:24:31  87df340098 "evening, he went into the large division of the tent at three o’clock in"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:25:33  8034916b7e "the morning, loudly blowing his nose. He asked whether the Russians had"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:27:47  189b00e2ac "not withdrawn, and was told that the enemy’s fires were still in the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:28:38  f1e41b09c2 "same places. He nodded approval."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:30:25  494fd31bf7 "The adjutant in attendance came into the tent."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:31:16  17329f20b7 "“Well, Rapp, do you think we shall do good business today?” Napoleon"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:33:08  13e0d1cfdc "asked him."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:33:49  560673dcc3 "“Without doubt, sire,” replied Rapp."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:36:03  d79789464c "Napoleon looked at him."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:38:15  a8ebedc656 "“Do you remember, sire, what you did me the honor to say at Smolénsk?”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:40:39  4e826482bc "continued Rapp. “The wine is drawn and must be drunk.”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:41:10  c0deace001 "Napoleon frowned and sat silent for a long time leaning his head on his"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:41:43  af9516d163 "hand."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:42:49  e5c0ed0b9b "“This poor army!” he suddenly remarked. “It has diminished greatly since"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:44:10  d34a86257f "Smolénsk. Fortune is frankly a courtesan, Rapp. I have always said so"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:45:34  7a27189ad5 "and I am beginning to experience it. But the Guards, Rapp, the Guards"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:47:16  cc10aab36d "are intact?” he remarked interrogatively."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:49:22  7a0abcb674 "“Yes, sire,” replied Rapp."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:50:09  792664ad80 "Napoleon took a lozenge, put it in his mouth, and glanced at his watch."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:51:44  78c9179b31 "He was not sleepy and it was still not nearly morning. It was impossible"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:52:24  78ddaba1cf "to give further orders for the sake of killing time, for the orders had"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:53:11  0a4d94c264 "all been given and were now being executed."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:54:45  5141ac10eb "“Have the biscuits and rice been served out to the regiments of the"
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:56:02  d9773647c7 "Guards?” asked Napoleon sternly."
 10/19/1812 Mon 11:58:22  4d3113be30 "“Yes, sire.”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 12:00:50  3478c91362 "“The rice too?”"
 10/19/1812 Mon 12:01:25  6397ae9933 "Rapp replied that he had given the Emperor’s order about the rice, but"
 10/19/1812 Mon 12:03:53  c0deace001 "Napoleon shook his head in dissatisfaction as if not believing that"
 10/19/1812 Mon 12:04:32  6e85752c14 "his order had been executed. An attendant came in with punch. Napoleon"
 10/19/1812 Mon 12:05:08  8db1dd1962 "ordered another glass to be brought for Rapp, and silently sipped his"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:03:28  f8e5af39fe "On entering the earthwork he noticed that there were men doing something"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:08:19  dbf5a910be "the earth wall with his back turned as if he were examining something"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:11:11  1f0e390bd4 "some men who were holding him by the arm. He also saw something else"
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:13:14  33c3896099 "that was strange."
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:15:29  203e883c4f "But he had not time to realize that the colonel had been killed, that"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:19:35  f6628cebb6 "had been bayoneted in the back before his eyes, for hardly had he run"
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:20:49  92eb500615 "into the redoubt before a thin, sallow-faced, perspiring man in a blue"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:28:17  b1411a5874 "the man (a French officer) by the shoulder with one hand and by the"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:30:47  89245285eb "his collar."
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:31:46  1f3ab3e9e8 "For some seconds they gazed with frightened eyes at one another’s"
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:34:13  bcad356282 "unfamiliar faces and both were perplexed at what they had done and"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:38:54  483fb8ef22 "hand, impelled by instinctive fear, squeezed his throat ever tighter and"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:54:43  57e8e9361d "it was the attack in which he was said to have thrown some St. George’s"

 10/19/1812 Mon 23:58:17  19cef61faa "take who got there.)"
 10/19/1812 Mon 23:59:55  498f46a152 "The French who had occupied the battery fled, and our troops shouting"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:02:02  4a0b0e9dbd "“Hurrah!” pursued them so far beyond the battery that it was difficult"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:03:48  3ed4eecf7b "to call them back."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:05:00  3e61a8db12 "The prisoners were brought down from the battery and among them was"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:06:36  77ec676ce0 "a wounded French general, whom the officers surrounded. Crowds of"

 10/20/1812 Tue 00:13:29  49b0782efa "he had spent over an hour, and of that family circle which had received"

 10/20/1812 Tue 00:25:46  21ce3fdb68 "Pierre ran down the slope once more."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:28:09  90a5d58ed5 "“Now they will stop it, now they will be horrified at what they have"

 10/20/1812 Tue 00:29:26  bf0d2aa15b "moving from the battlefield."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:30:00  71b729254e "But behind the veil of smoke the sun was still high, and in front and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:30:32  6d44121393 "especially to the left, near Semënovsk, something seemed to be seething"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:31:45  566a7e8862 "in the smoke, and the roar of cannon and musketry did not diminish, but"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:32:20  42658be23e "even increased to desperation like a man who, straining himself, shrieks"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:33:02  8877588b34 "with all his remaining strength."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:35:31  3d2ab303fb "CHAPTER XXXIII"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:36:48  fdc139a253 "The chief action of the battle of Borodinó was fought within the seven"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:38:09  3a5e50874f "thousand feet between Borodinó and Bagratión’s flèches. Beyond that"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:40:00  0a9fe59c58 "space there was, on the one side, a demonstration made by the Russians"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:41:24  f9343bc277 "with Uvárov’s cavalry at midday, and on the other side, beyond Utítsa,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:43:01  8afd723675 "Poniatowski’s collision with Túchkov; but these two were detached and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:45:27  c0deace001 "feeble actions in comparison with what took place in the center of the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:46:04  a37db7e9f7 "battlefield. On the field between Borodinó and the flèches, beside the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:48:07  08448f9144 "wood, the chief action of the day took place on an open space visible"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:48:38  1278ed8af1 "from both sides and was fought in the simplest and most artless way."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:49:49  a29bed0310 "The battle began on both sides with a cannonade from several hundred"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:50:51  a8320d2ddd "guns."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:51:51  33b8e835c2 "Then when the whole field was covered with smoke, two divisions,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:52:45  7457c00e2f "Campan’s and Dessaix’s, advanced from the French right, while Murat’s"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:55:14  4f9c27f1c7 "troops advanced on Borodinó from their left."
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:57:13  4a6a00cf20 "From the Shevárdino Redoubt where Napoleon was standing the flèches were"
 10/20/1812 Tue 00:59:31  c6cde96758 "two thirds of a mile away, and it was more than a mile as the crow flies"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:01:20  65aa9fa181 "to Borodinó, so that Napoleon could not see what was happening there,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:03:01  eb67cb81d7 "especially as the smoke mingling with the mist hid the whole locality."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:05:14  123fb278b6 "The soldiers of Dessaix’s division advancing against the flèches could"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:07:41  1cd13e7387 "only be seen till they had entered the hollow that lay between them and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:09:19  e707c0fac9 "the flèches. As soon as they had descended into that hollow, the smoke"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:11:25  c8e537f893 "of the guns and musketry on the flèches grew so dense that it covered"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:12:08  a72f6ef347 "the whole approach on that side of it. Through the smoke glimpses could"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:13:39  5b0d5d81e4 "be caught of something black—probably men—and at times the glint of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:15:41  4a64863cb0 "bayonets. But whether they were moving or stationary, whether they were"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:16:18  663ff228ca "French or Russian, could not be discovered from the Shevárdino Redoubt."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:18:24  ccb55b5f21 "The sun had risen brightly and its slanting rays struck straight into"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:20:31  0ce10a3582 "Napoleon’s face as, shading his eyes with his hand, he looked at the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:21:13  c0deace001 "flèches. The smoke spread out before them, and at times it looked as if"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:22:07  97e0333d87 "the smoke were moving, at times as if the troops moved. Sometimes shouts"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:23:32  deff6b80a1 "were heard through the firing, but it was impossible to tell what was"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:24:51  891686652b "being done there."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:26:31  4e77e0492a "Napoleon, standing on the knoll, looked through a field glass, and in"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:27:03  11a42ad957 "its small circlet saw smoke and men, sometimes his own and sometimes"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:28:10  b1b87a5e4f "Russians, but when he looked again with the naked eye, he could not tell"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:30:35  aa1c9dfe7f "where what he had seen was."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:31:14  ed68a6c83a "He descended the knoll and began walking up and down before it."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:31:47  9ca7ba21c0 "Occasionally he stopped, listened to the firing, and gazed intently at"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:34:05  8be09009ac "the battlefield."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:35:25  9c764fdbaf "But not only was it impossible to make out what was happening from where"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:36:30  92a86f1ed7 "he was standing down below, or from the knoll above on which some of his"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:37:11  25eeca0d6f "generals had taken their stand, but even from the flèches themselves—in"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:38:47  abfea6cb0c "which by this time there were now Russian and now French soldiers,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:39:51  84d1e2d717 "alternately or together, dead, wounded, alive, frightened, or"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:42:01  2e1a886f54 "maddened—even at those flèches themselves it was impossible to make out"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:43:25  9501b185c9 "what was taking place. There for several hours amid incessant cannon and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:45:40  5604b0f994 "musketry fire, now Russians were seen alone, now Frenchmen alone, now"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:47:01  3042d2c0ae "infantry, and now cavalry: they appeared, fired, fell, collided, not"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:48:08  b53a93aabc "knowing what to do with one another, screamed, and ran back again."
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:50:21  c0deace001 "From the battlefield adjutants he had sent out, and orderlies from his"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:50:56  5b41547f62 "marshals, kept galloping up to Napoleon with reports of the progress"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:53:14  4f046e80fb "of the action, but all these reports were false, both because it was"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:54:37  c1759b4be1 "impossible in the heat of battle to say what was happening at any given"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:56:44  f53e99de93 "moment and because many of the adjutants did not go to the actual place"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:59:02  8e7c5f0db7 "of conflict but reported what they had heard from others; and also"
 10/20/1812 Tue 01:59:53  6a19fa2b01 "because while an adjutant was riding more than a mile to Napoleon"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:01:29  e525677a98 "circumstances changed and the news he brought was already becoming"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:01:59  0d6142d521 "false. Thus an adjutant galloped up from Murat with tidings that"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:04:26  00425fe275 "Borodinó had been occupied and the bridge over the Kolochá was in the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:06:18  d27766186c "hands of the French. The adjutant asked whether Napoleon wished the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:07:43  4d2e26e4c2 "troops to cross it? Napoleon gave orders that the troops should form up"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:08:51  32f7670f65 "on the farther side and wait. But before that order was given—almost"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:09:53  cd9800c946 "as soon in fact as the adjutant had left Borodinó—the bridge had been"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:11:12  d4bbb0624e "retaken by the Russians and burned, in the very skirmish at which Pierre"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:12:58  9fb11a6869 "had been present at the beginning of the battle."
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:13:47  3a48953494 "An adjutant galloped up from the flèches with a pale and frightened face"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:15:15  1c93360dbb "and reported to Napoleon that their attack had been repulsed, Campan"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:17:04  80194daaeb "wounded, and Davout killed; yet at the very time the adjutant had been"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:17:42  e65b9d396c "told that the French had been repulsed, the flèches had in fact been"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:19:52  0489fa7b95 "recaptured by other French troops, and Davout was alive and only"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:22:08  0d2d336c9c "slightly bruised. On the basis of these necessarily untrustworthy"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:22:57  f34af4c23a "reports Napoleon gave his orders, which had either been executed before"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:24:05  17fd579647 "he gave them or could not be and were not executed."
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:24:55  36689fbf33 "The marshals and generals, who were nearer to the field of battle"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:27:16  3380e3ab5c "but, like Napoleon, did not take part in the actual fighting and only"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:29:18  653267ebf9 "occasionally went within musket range, made their own arrangements"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:31:46  b8bd2b2be0 "without asking Napoleon and issued orders where and in what direction to"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:32:58  135c2cb562 "fire and where cavalry should gallop and infantry should run. But even"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:33:30  6150a02562 "their orders, like Napoleon’s, were seldom carried out, and then but"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:35:41  4d6768d816 "partially. For the most part things happened contrary to their orders."
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:36:37  f4e0b59451 "Soldiers ordered to advance ran back on meeting grapeshot; soldiers"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:37:14  3c43aba4b4 "ordered to remain where they were, suddenly, seeing Russians"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:39:05  c0deace001 "unexpectedly before them, sometimes rushed back and sometimes forward,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:41:12  933390f763 "and the cavalry dashed without orders in pursuit of the flying Russians."
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:42:51  85f70c82e5 "In this way two cavalry regiments galloped through the Semënovsk hollow"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:44:53  d6d43725ae "and as soon as they reached the top of the incline turned round and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:46:06  5f51880839 "galloped full speed back again. The infantry moved in the same way,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:47:45  cf2590af93 "sometimes running to quite other places than those they were ordered to"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:49:37  398add792f "go to. All orders as to where and when to move the guns, when to send"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:50:13  85c798304c "infantry to shoot or horsemen to ride down the Russian infantry—all"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:52:39  92e8ecd9af "such orders were given by the officers on the spot nearest to the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:55:01  1678cc6dc4 "units concerned, without asking either Ney, Davout, or Murat, much less"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:56:01  9604117f9e "Napoleon. They did not fear getting into trouble for not fulfilling"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:57:08  8d089e44ab "orders or for acting on their own initiative, for in battle what is at"
 10/20/1812 Tue 02:58:46  3f9ca7b3b5 "stake is what is dearest to man—his own life—and it sometimes seems that"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:00:06  9bc6e4ec37 "safety lies in running back, sometimes in running forward; and these men"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:02:03  142628cd19 "who were right in the heat of the battle acted according to the mood"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:02:52  b996184f8f "of the moment. In reality, however, all these movements forward and"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:04:12  c0deace001 "backward did not improve or alter the position of the troops. All"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:04:47  4e8762786a "their rushing and galloping at one another did little harm, the harm of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:06:26  03e4d651d3 "disablement and death was caused by the balls and bullets that flew over"

 10/20/1812 Tue 03:09:29  80a86226e1 "left the place where the balls and bullets were flying about, their"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:10:59  fcad8d975d "superiors, located in the background, re-formed them and brought them"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:12:39  c0deace001 "under discipline and under the influence of that discipline led them"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:14:43  07ff0286fa "back to the zone of fire, where under the influence of fear of death"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:16:17  a155b4b479 "they lost their discipline and rushed about according to the chance"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:18:36  1685e06a1d "promptings of the throng."
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:20:58  a7e67f912a "CHAPTER XXXIV"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:22:39  41a2ab060d "Napoleon’s generals—Davout, Ney, and Murat, who were near that region of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:24:19  4e71484eec "fire and sometimes even entered it—repeatedly led into it huge masses of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:25:52  8041218a15 "well-ordered troops. But contrary to what had always happened in their"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:27:02  53e1e87d7c "former battles, instead of the news they expected of the enemy’s flight,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:27:44  c0deace001 "these orderly masses returned thence as disorganized and terrified mobs."
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:29:30  ac9d15da70 "The generals re-formed them, but their numbers constantly decreased."
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:31:13  1292f9820c "In the middle of the day Murat sent his adjutant to Napoleon to demand"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:33:25  168f0f21f1 "reinforcements."
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:35:09  2dc1f994e8 "Napoleon sat at the foot of the knoll, drinking punch, when Murat’s"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:36:49  66eadd1ef3 "adjutant galloped up with an assurance that the Russians would be routed"

 10/20/1812 Tue 03:52:10  7d1bef952a "The handsome boy adjutant with the long hair sighed deeply without"
 10/20/1812 Tue 03:52:57  88437f5178 "removing his hand from his hat and galloped back to where men were being"

 10/20/1812 Tue 03:56:51  8340f0faa0 "Napoleon rose and having summoned Caulaincourt and Berthier began"

 10/20/1812 Tue 04:25:46  b4ca385812 "“Asks for reinforcements?” said Napoleon with an angry gesture."
 10/20/1812 Tue 04:27:51  b07e555371 "The adjutant bent his head affirmatively and began to report, but the"

 10/20/1812 Tue 10:53:05  7c7245c8e1 "the exhausted, wavering men felt comforted and inspirited."
 10/20/1812 Tue 10:53:43  a2108f3913 "CHAPTER XXXVI"
 10/20/1812 Tue 10:55:09  621c928236 "Prince Andrew’s regiment was among the reserves which till after one"
 10/20/1812 Tue 10:57:14  54e9bc934c "o’clock were stationed inactive behind Semënovsk, under heavy artillery"
 10/20/1812 Tue 10:58:22  9ad86a3975 "fire. Toward two o’clock the regiment, having already lost more than"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:00:48  746110f816 "two hundred men, was moved forward into a trampled oatfield in the gap"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:01:20  677c120b93 "between Semënovsk and the Knoll Battery, where thousands of men perished"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:02:47  ad152df0cc "that day and on which an intense, concentrated fire from several hundred"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:03:46  ec4a7f92ff "enemy guns was directed between one and two o’clock."
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:06:14  1e25f78c44 "Without moving from that spot or firing a single shot the regiment here"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:08:05  11758950ca "lost another third of its men. From in front and especially from the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:10:24  67286457fb "right, in the unlifting smoke the guns boomed, and out of the mysterious"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:12:43  43fdb56acc "domain of smoke that overlay the whole space in front, quick hissing"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:15:03  92b5a0101c "cannon balls and slow whistling shells flew unceasingly. At times, as"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:15:46  c9bce73504 "if to allow them a respite, a quarter of an hour passed during which"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:17:30  1e644aa341 "the cannon balls and shells all flew overhead, but sometimes several men"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:19:30  82f72fd401 "were torn from the regiment in a minute and the slain were continually"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:21:51  ead65aa93a "being dragged away and the wounded carried off."
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:23:15  706c8b93b4 "With each fresh blow less and less chance of life remained for those not"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:24:43  46371c4e96 "yet killed. The regiment stood in columns of battalion, three hundred"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:25:27  30ce0f8baa "paces apart, but nevertheless the men were always in one and the same"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:26:02  bec99a68c8 "mood. All alike were taciturn and morose. Talk was rarely heard in the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:26:52  2fbd07adc8 "ranks, and it ceased altogether every time the thud of a successful"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:27:29  2c9cd8e2f7 "shot and the cry of “stretchers!” was heard. Most of the time, by their"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:28:34  d326607715 "officers’ order, the men sat on the ground. One, having taken off his"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:30:51  82ffc44e23 "shako, carefully loosened the gathers of its lining and drew them tight"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:33:05  f3a2098e52 "again; another, rubbing some dry clay between his palms, polished"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:34:31  c0deace001 "his bayonet; another fingered the strap and pulled the buckle of his"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:36:44  c70d69a7d6 "bandolier, while another smoothed and refolded his leg bands and put"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:39:00  dba8d17105 "his boots on again. Some built little houses of the tufts in the plowed"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:40:06  5d23526242 "ground, or plaited baskets from the straw in the cornfield. All seemed"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:42:20  488efd71cb "fully absorbed in these pursuits. When men were killed or wounded, when"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:43:24  5b444fc1b8 "rows of stretchers went past, when some troops retreated, and when great"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:43:58  3f375ce110 "masses of the enemy came into view through the smoke, no one paid any"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:44:50  503b7859ca "attention to these things. But when our artillery or cavalry advanced or"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:45:51  8a6ec84c61 "some of our infantry were seen to move forward, words of approval"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:46:27  8f17436013 "were heard on all sides. But the liveliest attention was attracted by"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:48:08  6d44528723 "occurrences quite apart from, and unconnected with, the battle. It was"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:49:30  362840cd01 "as if the minds of these morally exhausted men found relief in everyday,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:50:04  83da1b1d39 "commonplace occurrences. A battery of artillery was passing in front of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:51:06  be84493e0d "the regiment. The horse of an ammunition cart put its leg over a trace."
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:52:17  ec89ab2c7e "“Hey, look at the trace horse!... Get her leg out! She’ll fall.... Ah,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:54:32  33ee7e1a4f "they don’t see it!” came identical shouts from the ranks all along the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:55:16  6c6198391c "regiment. Another time, general attention was attracted by a small brown"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:56:40  c9554b04a0 "dog, coming heaven knows whence, which trotted in a preoccupied manner"
 10/20/1812 Tue 11:58:01  621f612c17 "in front of the ranks with tail stiffly erect till suddenly a shell fell"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:00:15  4f65c37ebb "close by, when it yelped, tucked its tail between its legs, and darted"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:01:23  c0deace001 "aside. Yells and shrieks of laughter rose from the whole regiment. But"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:02:35  19b7353418 "such distractions lasted only a moment, and for eight hours the men had"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:03:57  25b95765b5 "been inactive, without food, in constant fear of death, and their pale"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:06:10  32a04746b5 "and gloomy faces grew ever paler and gloomier."
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:07:35  950946785f "Prince Andrew, pale and gloomy like everyone in the regiment, paced up"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:08:56  a927bf6741 "and down from the border of one patch to another, at the edge of the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:09:36  cd4547b3e3 "meadow beside an oatfield, with head bowed and arms behind his back."
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:10:48  5197de4e30 "There was nothing for him to do and no orders to be given. Everything"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:11:54  a239539154 "went on of itself. The killed were dragged from the front, the wounded"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:13:23  c0deace001 "carried away, and the ranks closed up. If any soldiers ran to the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:14:04  c968ce2516 "rear they returned immediately and hastily. At first Prince Andrew,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:15:19  f36d162d2d "considering it his duty to rouse the courage of the men and to set them"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:17:33  56e24b73e1 "an example, walked about among the ranks, but he soon became convinced"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:19:58  1ba02fea40 "that this was unnecessary and that there was nothing he could teach"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:21:47  e4347818fb "them. All the powers of his soul, as of every soldier there, were"

 10/20/1812 Tue 12:29:04  bd4c655da9 "strides trying to keep to the footprints left on the meadow by the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:30:55  e75a402ef0 "mowers, then he counted his steps, calculating how often he must walk"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:31:59  4a93df64e9 "from one strip to another to walk a mile, then he stripped the flowers"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:34:11  c9c3e25f73 "from the wormwood that grew along a boundary rut, rubbed them in his"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:36:34  a7011bceb3 "palms, and smelled their pungent, sweetly bitter scent. Nothing remained"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:38:11  576eb34d43 "of the previous day’s thoughts. He thought of nothing. He listened with"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:40:00  89af42867f "weary ears to the ever-recurring sounds, distinguishing the whistle"

 10/20/1812 Tue 12:47:16  1d125777d7 "it has gone over. But this one has hit!” And again he started trying"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:48:13  f61591f0b3 "to reach the boundary strip in sixteen paces. A whizz and a thud! Five"

 10/20/1812 Tue 12:51:52  7f6a9c96ae "chill ran down his back. Again he glanced at the ranks. Probably many"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:53:44  bbb2b1ca79 "had been hit—a large crowd had gathered near the second battalion."
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:54:22  5bead45793 "“Adjutant!” he shouted. “Order them not to crowd together.”"
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:56:17  aad9150e88 "The adjutant, having obeyed this instruction, approached Prince Andrew."
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:58:43  841adbebe0 "From the other side a battalion commander rode up."
 10/20/1812 Tue 12:59:49  953991f9a2 "“Look out!” came a frightened cry from a soldier and, like a bird"

 10/20/1812 Tue 17:36:17  eaf7aa4bf1 "CHAPTER XXXVIII"
 10/20/1812 Tue 17:37:10  c0deace001 "The terrible spectacle of the battlefield covered with dead and wounded,"
