 10/20/1812 Tue 22:51:40  712c4faac6 "BOOK ELEVEN: 1812"
 10/20/1812 Tue 22:52:45  e887626ba7 "CHAPTER I"
 10/20/1812 Tue 22:54:50  475cac02d3 "Absolute continuity of motion is not comprehensible to the human mind."
 10/20/1812 Tue 22:57:06  0258c37690 "Laws of motion of any kind become comprehensible to man only when he"
 10/20/1812 Tue 22:59:04  abb0af7a21 "examines arbitrarily selected elements of that motion; but at the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:00:02  15fed8a169 "same time, a large proportion of human error comes from the arbitrary"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:01:33  6bb2849367 "division of continuous motion into discontinuous elements. There is a"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:03:26  fdca406e5e "well-known, so-called sophism of the ancients consisting in this, that"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:04:14  86fb29966f "Achilles could never catch up with a tortoise he was following, in spite"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:06:41  812e7d3a64 "of the fact that he traveled ten times as fast as the tortoise. By"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:08:08  e9375e2940 "the time Achilles has covered the distance that separated him from the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:09:03  575ea49e54 "tortoise, the tortoise has covered one tenth of that distance ahead"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:10:48  be2f59c156 "of him: when Achilles has covered that tenth, the tortoise has covered"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:12:09  3cbce73283 "another one hundredth, and so on forever. This problem seemed to"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:13:46  fbf2064f89 "the ancients insoluble. The absurd answer (that Achilles could never"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:14:33  4e1d5fe519 "overtake the tortoise) resulted from this: that motion was arbitrarily"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:16:01  d8f6e245de "divided into discontinuous elements, whereas the motion both of Achilles"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:18:24  af1c3aea18 "and of the tortoise was continuous."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:20:26  bba23ef782 "By adopting smaller and smaller elements of motion we only approach a"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:22:48  07a6d8329f "solution of the problem, but never reach it. Only when we have admitted"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:24:14  a1b89e4991 "the conception of the infinitely small, and the resulting geometrical"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:25:16  a924c66c5b "progression with a common ratio of one tenth, and have found the sum of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:26:54  cda25b06cd "this progression to infinity, do we reach a solution of the problem."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:27:24  eac340328f "A modern branch of mathematics having achieved the art of dealing with"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:28:52  f39bc58960 "the infinitely small can now yield solutions in other more complex"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:30:10  b5a2d0e25d "problems of motion which used to appear insoluble."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:31:14  d8106e7f40 "This modern branch of mathematics, unknown to the ancients, when dealing"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:32:26  50e83b9344 "with problems of motion admits the conception of the infinitely small,"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:34:37  c0deace001 "and so conforms to the chief condition of motion (absolute continuity)"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:35:32  706ac1d2b0 "and thereby corrects the inevitable error which the human mind cannot"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:37:49  8d8224a58b "avoid when it deals with separate elements of motion instead of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:39:16  b22973cc75 "examining continuous motion."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:39:47  9d62cbf681 "In seeking the laws of historical movement just the same thing happens."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:41:50  eb88488346 "The movement of humanity, arising as it does from innumerable arbitrary"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:42:45  0eda29d880 "human wills, is continuous."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:43:44  7f430977fc "To understand the laws of this continuous movement is the aim of"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:44:40  38b2e5ef0a "history. But to arrive at these laws, resulting from the sum of all"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:46:51  ca64cbe047 "those human wills, man’s mind postulates arbitrary and disconnected"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:48:08  c0deace001 "units. The first method of history is to take an arbitrarily selected"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:49:16  f1cec56d70 "series of continuous events and examine it apart from others, though"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:50:51  ef24dce4b0 "there is and can be no beginning to any event, for one event always"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:52:52  508d7ae911 "flows uninterruptedly from another."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:54:44  d210e98d1f "The second method is to consider the actions of some one man—a king or a"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:55:26  ec856869ad "commander—as equivalent to the sum of many individual wills; whereas the"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:57:45  4860d71c59 "sum of individual wills is never expressed by the activity of a single"
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:58:27  eb3687c253 "historic personage."
 10/20/1812 Tue 23:59:02  fe29fdff36 "Historical science in its endeavor to draw nearer to truth continually"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:00:45  83524dfda9 "takes smaller and smaller units for examination. But however small the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:03:11  23ddfd9657 "units it takes, we feel that to take any unit disconnected from others,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:04:35  4e6bed7983 "or to assume a beginning of any phenomenon, or to say that the will of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:06:50  92965cba7f "many men is expressed by the actions of any one historic personage, is"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:08:25  b290fb3bf4 "in itself false."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:09:49  03544a37ac "It needs no critical exertion to reduce utterly to dust any deductions"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:10:54  39b02eccb5 "drawn from history. It is merely necessary to select some larger or"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:13:17  3c0c48555d "smaller unit as the subject of observation—as criticism has every"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:15:08  12e131b013 "right to do, seeing that whatever unit history observes must always be"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:16:55  f2c7ca593e "arbitrarily selected."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:18:59  e19d083f66 "Only by taking infinitesimally small units for observation (the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:21:20  c0deace001 "differential of history, that is, the individual tendencies of men) and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:23:11  b8e918a545 "attaining to the art of integrating them (that is, finding the sum of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:24:21  1c16f51e81 "these infinitesimals) can we hope to arrive at the laws of history."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:26:26  51a363ae85 "The first fifteen years of the nineteenth century in Europe present an"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:27:43  3ae2ecf50d "extraordinary movement of millions of people. Men leave their customary"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:29:10  50ccc2e1b5 "pursuits, hasten from one side of Europe to the other, plunder and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:31:36  6f7fe5cced "slaughter one another, triumph and are plunged in despair, and for some"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:33:19  dda27fd670 "years the whole course of life is altered and presents an intensive"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:34:27  9f5157dbfe "movement which first increases and then slackens. What was the cause of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:35:33  111bb9aa97 "this movement, by what laws was it governed? asks the mind of man."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:37:32  b59cfbb27f "The historians, replying to this question, lay before us the sayings and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:39:11  5a0e5a087a "doings of a few dozen men in a building in the city of Paris, calling"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:41:22  784e10bef5 "these sayings and doings “the Revolution”; then they give a detailed"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:42:53  ff5a615e5e "biography of Napoleon and of certain people favorable or hostile to him;"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:43:54  845ef347db "tell of the influence some of these people had on others, and say: that"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:46:09  d3a85d95ad "is why this movement took place and those are its laws."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:47:21  177943ef4d "But the mind of man not only refuses to believe this explanation, but"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:48:34  84c55cb134 "plainly says that this method of explanation is fallacious, because in"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:50:46  9e3545b7d7 "it a weaker phenomenon is taken as the cause of a stronger. The sum of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:53:11  efb77b1ea9 "human wills produced the Revolution and Napoleon, and only the sum of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:54:20  70ad584bcd "those wills first tolerated and then destroyed them."
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:55:26  afad9753f8 "“But every time there have been conquests there have been conquerors;"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:57:28  48535e8b28 "every time there has been a revolution in any state there have been"
 10/21/1812 Wed 00:59:42  7b0055a456 "great men,” says history. And, indeed, human reason replies: every time"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:01:35  c0deace001 "conquerors appear there have been wars, but this does not prove that the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:03:42  374b0a1d09 "conquerors caused the wars and that it is possible to find the laws of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:04:56  7b6b7e2506 "a war in the personal activity of a single man. Whenever I look at my"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:06:42  45ac12983d "watch and its hands point to ten, I hear the bells of the neighboring"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:08:15  143d717b04 "church; but because the bells begin to ring when the hands of the clock"

 10/21/1812 Wed 01:11:27  e6a8eed9ca "Whenever I see the movement of a locomotive I hear the whistle and see"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:13:04  3fd334ba76 "the valves opening and wheels turning; but I have no right to conclude"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:13:52  0eccc240bb "that the whistling and the turning of wheels are the cause of the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:15:34  148cb3198f "movement of the engine."
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:16:08  c0deace001 "The peasants say that a cold wind blows in late spring because the oaks"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:16:55  ab3714443b "are budding, and really every spring cold winds do blow when the oak"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:18:00  478473e234 "is budding. But though I do not know what causes the cold winds to blow"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:19:20  8c28140a3d "when the oak buds unfold, I cannot agree with the peasants that the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:21:37  211639ec57 "unfolding of the oak buds is the cause of the cold wind, for the"

 10/21/1812 Wed 01:34:53  9a0b1b00d0 "direction have already been made."
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:36:44  66e4a834ca "To study the laws of history we must completely change the subject of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:37:33  bc75c453e3 "our observation, must leave aside kings, ministers, and generals, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:38:52  f809596d79 "study the common, infinitesimally small elements by which the masses are"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:40:20  dffad15bc8 "moved. No one can say in how far it is possible for man to advance"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:42:24  5f4d8009f6 "in this way toward an understanding of the laws of history; but it is"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:43:42  c99be99c93 "evident that only along that path does the possibility of discovering"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:44:39  dbfcb120f2 "the laws of history lie, and that as yet not a millionth part as much"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:45:27  8ebb736aef "mental effort has been applied in this direction by historians as has"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:47:53  2729c809ea "been devoted to describing the actions of various kings, commanders,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:49:54  73915aad56 "and ministers and propounding the historians’ own reflections concerning"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:51:09  9c4cb29b6a "these actions."
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:52:25  c0deace001 "CHAPTER II"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:54:39  9ef391aaa8 "The forces of a dozen European nations burst into Russia. The Russian"
 10/21/1812 Wed 01:56:13  dcd0123841 "army and people avoided a collision till Smolénsk was reached, and again"

 10/21/1812 Wed 02:04:39  8cd2333d6c "Napoleon’s army felt this and the invasion moved on by its own momentum."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:06:13  b974cffae1 "The more the Russian army retreated the more fiercely a spirit of hatred"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:08:35  5dd9df55c9 "of the enemy flared up, and while it retreated the army increased and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:09:30  31cd87c87e "consolidated. At Borodinó a collision took place. Neither army was"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:11:44  e3511da7ac "broken up, but the Russian army retreated immediately after the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:14:13  14f45035eb "collision as inevitably as a ball recoils after colliding with another"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:15:16  72b133459f "having a greater momentum, and with equal inevitability the ball"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:16:52  7f53d06fbf "of invasion that had advanced with such momentum rolled on for some"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:18:03  c717237d41 "distance, though the collision had deprived it of all its force."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:18:49  90cf280433 "The Russians retreated eighty miles—to beyond Moscow—and the French"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:19:42  4ed8ae565f "reached Moscow and there came to a standstill. For five weeks after that"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:20:14  1666240ad4 "there was not a single battle. The French did not move. As a bleeding,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:21:12  93f7320471 "mortally wounded animal licks its wounds, they remained inert in Moscow"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:22:46  ca389f76f5 "for five weeks, and then suddenly, with no fresh reason, fled back:"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:24:16  f050f1837c "they made a dash for the Kalúga road, and (after a victory—for at"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:24:48  1c00982067 "Málo-Yaroslávets the field of conflict again remained theirs) without"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:27:02  782e02f193 "undertaking a single serious battle, they fled still more rapidly back"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:28:52  d191da6889 "to Smolénsk, beyond Smolénsk, beyond the Berëzina, beyond Vílna, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:29:43  f568c27910 "farther still."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:31:53  e1330f09ea "On the evening of the twenty-sixth of August, Kutúzov and the whole"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:33:14  12fca53c82 "Russian army were convinced that the battle of Borodinó was a victory."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:34:42  16ed57f93c "Kutúzov reported so to the Emperor. He gave orders to prepare for a"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:35:39  1a06927ef5 "fresh conflict to finish the enemy and did this not to deceive anyone,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:36:48  245369ed4e "but because he knew that the enemy was beaten, as everyone who had taken"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:37:53  c0deace001 "part in the battle knew it."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:39:54  23766c3c21 "But all that evening and next day reports came in one after another"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:40:32  892ed38740 "of unheard-of losses, of the loss of half the army, and a fresh battle"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:41:36  ca698c8505 "proved physically impossible."
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:42:46  76c9cdc60f "It was impossible to give battle before information had been collected,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:43:32  3cdf9ad5fd "the wounded gathered in, the supplies of ammunition replenished, the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:44:30  35fd14408e "slain reckoned up, new officers appointed to replace those who had been"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:46:37  56ceadbf5d "killed, and before the men had had food and sleep. And meanwhile, the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:47:15  54fdbf708b "very next morning after the battle, the French army advanced of itself"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:48:38  cb008e3ae4 "upon the Russians, carried forward by the force of its own momentum now"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:50:29  9930979d6f "seemingly increased in inverse proportion to the square of the distance"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:52:58  9d6a381cf0 "from its aim. Kutúzov’s wish was to attack next day, and the whole"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:54:46  2422c8f52c "army desired to do so. But to make an attack the wish to do so is not"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:55:44  9009694c64 "sufficient, there must also be a possibility of doing it, and that"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:56:54  a841fff44e "possibility did not exist. It was impossible not to retreat a day’s"
 10/21/1812 Wed 02:58:51  24d8fa4936 "march, and then in the same way it was impossible not to retreat another"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:00:04  1212468c91 "and a third day’s march, and at last, on the first of September when"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:01:08  076abeafb4 "the army drew near Moscow—despite the strength of the feeling that had"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:03:33  1e50545d4a "arisen in all ranks—the force of circumstances compelled it to retire"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:05:43  77dea07c8d "beyond Moscow. And the troops retired one more, last, day’s march, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:07:40  7b8bd44285 "abandoned Moscow to the enemy."
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:09:59  b21816cc90 "For people accustomed to think that plans of campaign and battles are"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:11:53  d9a1f0ed7a "made by generals—as anyone of us sitting over a map in his study may"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:13:10  01068995ab "imagine how he would have arranged things in this or that battle—the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:13:50  cf5910d639 "questions present themselves: Why did Kutúzov during the retreat not do"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:15:25  877f9074d3 "this or that? Why did he not take up a position before reaching Filí?"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:17:33  f34c433ae3 "Why did he not retire at once by the Kalúga road, abandoning Moscow? and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:19:04  a919cd84df "so on. People accustomed to think in that way forget, or do not know,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:20:58  c0deace001 "the inevitable conditions which always limit the activities of any"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:22:56  256aae2987 "commander in chief. The activity of a commander in chief does not at all"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:24:05  80ee40ca24 "resemble the activity we imagine to ourselves when we sit at ease in"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:26:15  dc6d6962b6 "our studies examining some campaign on the map, with a certain number of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:28:21  ab01711936 "troops on this and that side in a certain known locality, and begin our"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:30:05  4a81511ef0 "plans from some given moment. A commander in chief is never dealing with"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:30:55  71b8804545 "the beginning of any event—the position from which we always contemplate"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:33:09  21cd7fc136 "it. The commander in chief is always in the midst of a series of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:35:13  9950b242e1 "shifting events and so he never can at any moment consider the whole"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:37:40  4905b76e3a "import of an event that is occurring. Moment by moment the event is"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:40:02  1b46b7bc40 "imperceptibly shaping itself, and at every moment of this continuous,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:40:51  a378d8e3fe "uninterrupted shaping of events the commander in chief is in the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:42:40  2df2662dd1 "midst of a most complex play of intrigues, worries, contingencies,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:44:53  f2e4b04c24 "authorities, projects, counsels, threats, and deceptions and is"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:47:00  fe0ce50b4d "continually obliged to reply to innumerable questions addressed to him,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:49:09  08ff161719 "which constantly conflict with one another."
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:50:02  e77e96b182 "Learned military authorities quite seriously tell us that Kutúzov should"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:51:28  8f83cb01c7 "have moved his army to the Kalúga road long before reaching Filí, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:52:12  ea40a54d20 "that somebody actually submitted such a proposal to him. But a commander"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:53:39  538dbd3cb4 "in chief, especially at a difficult moment, has always before him not"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:55:00  5630012c91 "one proposal but dozens simultaneously. And all these proposals, based"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:57:24  f0587ebd4d "on strategics and tactics, contradict each other."
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:58:18  fd2dc61154 "A commander in chief’s business, it would seem, is simply to choose one"
 10/21/1812 Wed 03:59:29  922ba7f0ab "of these projects. But even that he cannot do. Events and time do not"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:01:18  83ccd564c2 "wait. For instance, on the twenty-eighth it is suggested to him to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:02:59  d1af35d477 "cross to the Kalúga road, but just then an adjutant gallops up from"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:04:12  63a374b07d "Milorádovich asking whether he is to engage the French or retire. An"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:05:06  560574b853 "order must be given him at once, that instant. And the order to retreat"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:06:17  c2f5992431 "carries us past the turn to the Kalúga road. And after the adjutant"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:08:23  0374fb315e "comes the commissary general asking where the stores are to be taken,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:10:33  b57a40560a "and the chief of the hospitals asks where the wounded are to go, and a"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:11:53  128882a852 "courier from Petersburg brings a letter from the sovereign which does"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:13:19  3c036b3ec6 "not admit of the possibility of abandoning Moscow, and the commander in"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:14:08  fddfd46a1d "chief’s rival, the man who is undermining him (and there are always"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:15:08  9de525d434 "not merely one but several such), presents a new project diametrically"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:16:02  6e12563a5f "opposed to that of turning to the Kalúga road, and the commander in"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:17:57  fa59ab726a "chief himself needs sleep and refreshment to maintain his energy and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:19:10  c0deace001 "a respectable general who has been overlooked in the distribution of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:20:39  f669d60c33 "rewards comes to complain, and the inhabitants of the district pray to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:21:49  edec8f3b30 "be defended, and an officer sent to inspect the locality comes in and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:24:11  c71d9546ef "gives a report quite contrary to what was said by the officer"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:25:59  5128c5bcd2 "previously sent; and a spy, a prisoner, and a general who has been"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:28:20  1d0a2eb56a "on reconnaissance, all describe the position of the enemy’s army"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:30:25  e0d22c2d75 "differently. People accustomed to misunderstand or to forget these"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:31:43  341d3739ff "inevitable conditions of a commander in chief’s actions describe to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:33:35  c6f7937f5e "us, for instance, the position of the army at Filí and assume that the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:36:03  f4f3bf9558 "commander in chief could, on the first of September, quite freely decide"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:38:17  621226643d "whether to abandon Moscow or defend it; whereas, with the Russian army"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:40:24  c0deace001 "less than four miles from Moscow, no such question existed. When had"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:41:22  e6fdaa9110 "that question been settled? At Drissa and at Smolénsk and most"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:43:23  cf1817ed77 "palpably of all on the twenty-fourth of August at Shevárdino and on"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:44:57  6c389fb53a "the twenty-sixth at Borodinó, and each day and hour and minute of the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:46:28  fde9549a25 "retreat from Borodinó to Filí."
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:47:40  d9c275ca2b "CHAPTER III"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:48:18  abb950886c "When Ermólov, having been sent by Kutúzov to inspect the position, told"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:50:24  595b30d434 "the field marshal that it was impossible to fight there before Moscow"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:51:52  415484f68b "and that they must retreat, Kutúzov looked at him in silence."
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:53:11  9fcbb604e9 "“Give me your hand,” said he and, turning it over so as to feel the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:54:46  c8f125fbbb "pulse, added: “You are not well, my dear fellow. Think what you are"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:55:54  0251037633 "saying!”"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:57:56  825e012d3b "Kutúzov could not yet admit the possibility of retreating beyond Moscow"
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:58:27  67ed158e54 "without a battle."
 10/21/1812 Wed 04:59:55  5654230267 "On the Poklónny Hill, four miles from the Dorogomílov gate of Moscow,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:00:27  995a181e61 "Kutúzov got out of his carriage and sat down on a bench by the roadside."
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:01:23  4cf84b3235 "A great crowd of generals gathered round him, and Count Rostopchín, who"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:02:16  b522416e97 "had come out from Moscow, joined them. This brilliant company separated"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:03:23  f373d13440 "into several groups who all discussed the advantages and disadvantages"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:04:19  d1ac52d4b7 "of the position, the state of the army, the plans suggested, the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:06:12  394c73aec3 "situation of Moscow, and military questions generally. Though they had"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:08:00  da47412d34 "not been summoned for the purpose, and though it was not so called, they"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:08:49  91416db0c9 "all felt that this was really a council of war. The conversations all"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:09:52  cb0a63af4c "dealt with public questions. If anyone gave or asked for personal"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:11:23  553c774e14 "news, it was done in a whisper and they immediately reverted to general"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:13:47  8879327869 "matters. No jokes, or laughter, or smiles even, were seen among all"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:15:30  d5fdb811d7 "these men. They evidently all made an effort to hold themselves at the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:16:24  894368502f "height the situation demanded. And all these groups, while talking"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:18:39  3bcf981310 "among themselves, tried to keep near the commander in chief (whose"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:20:07  20ee6e5d33 "bench formed the center of the gathering) and to speak so that he might"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:22:30  9402b8b4d8 "overhear them. The commander in chief listened to what was being said"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:23:25  0dfaa4ad8b "and sometimes asked them to repeat their remarks, but did not himself"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:25:13  2844619b85 "take part in the conversations or express any opinion. After hearing"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:26:59  138c641557 "what was being said by one or other of these groups he generally turned"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:28:58  59b9812a96 "away with an air of disappointment, as though they were not speaking of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:29:39  bf69dff7a4 "anything he wished to hear. Some discussed the position that had been"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:32:08  c0deace001 "chosen, criticizing not the position itself so much as the mental"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:34:25  5463c53e11 "capacity of those who had chosen it. Others argued that a mistake had"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:35:52  ee191115b3 "been made earlier and that a battle should have been fought two days"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:36:41  1329787d52 "before. Others again spoke of the battle of Salamanca, which was"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:37:55  ede08ca401 "described by Crosart, a newly arrived Frenchman in a Spanish uniform."
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:40:01  bd99f78d08 "(This Frenchman and one of the German princes serving with the Russian"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:42:22  bcdc465727 "army were discussing the siege of Saragossa and considering the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:43:38  87730dfc23 "possibility of defending Moscow in a similar manner.) Count Rostopchín"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:44:34  b7ffa6b6ab "was telling a fourth group that he was prepared to die with the city"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:46:49  84abce8b4b "train bands under the walls of the capital, but that he still could not"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:48:23  1e99c305b1 "help regretting having been left in ignorance of what was happening, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:49:42  96b015c8a7 "that had he known it sooner things would have been different.... A"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:50:35  69f86689cb "fifth group, displaying the profundity of their strategic perceptions,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:52:35  20d8638d3e "discussed the direction the troops would now have to take. A sixth group"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:53:09  fd40dfb5b6 "was talking absolute nonsense. Kutúzov’s expression grew more and more"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:55:20  22429366c7 "preoccupied and gloomy. From all this talk he saw only one thing: that"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:57:31  0be814f50a "to defend Moscow was a physical impossibility in the full meaning of"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:58:31  83b432656d "those words, that is to say, so utterly impossible that if any senseless"
 10/21/1812 Wed 05:59:35  29a13eadb6 "commander were to give orders to fight, confusion would result but the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:01:33  5955323cd0 "battle would still not take place. It would not take place because the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:03:46  b3517de75e "commanders not merely all recognized the position to be impossible, but"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:05:06  e346f4082c "in their conversations were only discussing what would happen after its"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:06:41  e052b4c042 "inevitable abandonment. How could the commanders lead their troops to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:07:44  7108b663f6 "a field of battle they considered impossible to hold? The lower-grade"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:08:57  814377337f "officers and even the soldiers (who too reason) also considered the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:10:57  fb5f128403 "position impossible and therefore could not go to fight, fully convinced"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:13:18  c0deace001 "as they were of defeat. If Bennigsen insisted on the position being"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:14:39  4017353c93 "defended and others still discussed it, the question was no longer"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:15:11  8df2f5e12f "important in itself but only as a pretext for disputes and intrigue."
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:17:32  9a2f557da7 "This Kutúzov knew well."
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:18:23  185828fcb2 "Bennigsen, who had chosen the position, warmly displayed his Russian"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:20:35  fc9e4d5b10 "patriotism (Kutúzov could not listen to this without wincing) by"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:21:45  510147079e "insisting that Moscow must be defended. His aim was as clear as daylight"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:22:55  76f225ab69 "to Kutúzov: if the defense failed, to throw the blame on Kutúzov who had"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:23:43  30ebb12515 "brought the army as far as the Sparrow Hills without giving battle; if"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:24:21  c644b84a42 "it succeeded, to claim the success as his own; or if battle were not"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:25:22  0b4f70855a "given, to clear himself of the crime of abandoning Moscow. But this"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:26:56  529f6fa2f3 "intrigue did not now occupy the old man’s mind. One terrible question"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:28:00  5b82817f57 "absorbed him and to that question he heard no reply from anyone. The"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:28:38  f2e64fcc81 "question for him now was: “Have I really allowed Napoleon to reach"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:29:08  9243677685 "Moscow, and when did I do so? When was it decided? Can it have been"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:30:54  12e92d0991 "yesterday when I ordered Plátov to retreat, or was it the evening"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:31:55  c0deace001 "before, when I had a nap and told Bennigsen to issue orders? Or was it"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:33:45  7859c97635 "earlier still?... When, when was this terrible affair decided? Moscow"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:34:19  0c025387e6 "must be abandoned. The army must retreat and the order to do so must"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:35:53  c0deace001 "be given.” To give that terrible order seemed to him equivalent to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:37:02  894803044a "resigning the command of the army. And not only did he love power to"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:37:56  387615f628 "which he was accustomed (the honours awarded to Prince Prozoróvski,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:39:52  38d4040287 "under whom he had served in Turkey, galled him), but he was convinced"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:41:51  d59093fa7d "that he was destined to save Russia and that that was why, against"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:43:50  cf6910f6ba "the Emperor’s wish and by the will of the people, he had been chosen"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:46:19  ca51558c98 "commander in chief. He was convinced that he alone could maintain"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:46:54  a84996b456 "command of the army in these difficult circumstances, and that in all"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:48:15  1bdb3352e2 "the world he alone could encounter the invincible Napoleon without fear,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:50:28  c0deace001 "and he was horrified at the thought of the order he had to issue. But"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:52:41  5828df5401 "something had to be decided, and these conversations around him which"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:54:48  7141b1fb5e "were assuming too free a character must be stopped."
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:56:58  a708c7627e "He called the most important generals to him."
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:57:32  97dea19172 "“My head, be it good or bad, must depend on itself,” said he, rising"
 10/21/1812 Wed 06:59:13  f3747cf957 "from the bench, and he rode to Filí where his carriages were waiting."
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:00:03  8c464678de "CHAPTER IV"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:01:09  3628549da1 "The Council of War began to assemble at two in the afternoon in the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:03:09  b4cfe85633 "better and roomier part of Andrew Savostyánov’s hut. The men, women, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:04:00  5517540a9b "children of the large peasant family crowded into the back room across"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:05:29  7eff3bf775 "the passage. Only Malásha, Andrew’s six-year-old granddaughter whom"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:06:25  fd524f2eca "his Serene Highness had petted and to whom he had given a lump of sugar"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:07:42  c0deace001 "while drinking his tea, remained on the top of the brick oven in the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:08:31  1d8a417f9d "larger room. Malásha looked down from the oven with shy delight at the"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:09:04  232903ad32 "faces, uniforms, and decorations of the generals, who one after another"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:11:13  e7561e4abf "came into the room and sat down on the broad benches in the corner"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:13:25  f20f331c78 "under the icons. “Granddad” himself, as Malásha in her own mind called"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:15:11  22328a98c3 "Kutúzov, sat apart in a dark corner behind the oven. He sat, sunk deep"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:17:24  a9bb42264e "in a folding armchair, and continually cleared his throat and pulled at"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:18:32  6f1800edf4 "the collar of his coat which, though it was unbuttoned, still seemed"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:20:00  93bcb6c363 "to pinch his neck. Those who entered went up one by one to the field"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:20:44  823e985b21 "marshal; he pressed the hands of some and nodded to others. His adjutant"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:22:17  b286ebac57 "Kaysárov was about to draw back the curtain of the window facing"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:23:03  5bc3a20a4e "Kutúzov, but the latter moved his hand angrily and Kaysárov understood"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:25:09  a50786e9ab "that his Serene Highness did not wish his face to be seen."
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:26:03  0b1e0a0171 "Round the peasant’s deal table, on which lay maps, plans, pencils, and"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:26:49  b0ff8abc00 "papers, so many people gathered that the orderlies brought in another"
 10/21/1812 Wed 07:29:00  55557b3306 "bench and put it beside the table. Ermólov, Kaysárov, and Toll, who had"

 10/21/1812 Wed 09:55:48  61d02fdde9 "CHAPTER V"
 10/21/1812 Wed 09:57:31  d03d558858 "At that very time, in circumstances even more important than retreating"
 10/21/1812 Wed 09:58:43  2fb0846659 "without a battle, namely the evacuation and burning of Moscow,"
 10/21/1812 Wed 10:00:02  f20cb1d840 "Rostopchín, who is usually represented as being the instigator of that"

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:04:29  f58f148150 "After the battle of Borodinó the abandonment and burning of Moscow was"

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:10:32  61e590a7c4 "The same thing that took place in Moscow had happened in all the towns"

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:21:20  9b8ca36511 "while the poorer remained and burned and destroyed what was left."

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:27:20  588f1ecea1 "and a foreboding that Moscow would be taken, was present in Russian"
 10/21/1812 Wed 10:27:50  3334e04d8c "Moscow society in 1812. Those who had quitted Moscow already in July"

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:40:22  c530464468 "“It is disgraceful to run away from danger; only cowards are running"

 10/21/1812 Wed 10:44:55  71f18810dd "impressed on them that to leave Moscow was shameful. They were ashamed"
 10/21/1812 Wed 10:45:56  c0218764e5 "to be called cowards, ashamed to leave, but still they left, knowing"
